-- TOC entry 238 (class 1255 OID 16725)
-- Name: add_group(text, text[]); Type: FUNCTION; Schema: public; Owner: postgres
--

CREATE FUNCTION public.add_group(name text, words text[]) RETURNS void
    LANGUAGE sql
    AS $$insert into words
select unnest(words)
on conflict(word) do nothing;

INSERT INTO public.groups(name)
values(name);

insert into public.words_in_groups
select name as group_name, unnest(words) as word

$$;


ALTER FUNCTION public.add_group(name text, words text[]) OWNER TO postgres;

--
-- TOC entry 254 (class 1255 OID 16805)
-- Name: filtersongs(text, text, text[]); Type: FUNCTION; Schema: public; Owner: postgres
--

CREATE FUNCTION public.filtersongs(_name text, _artist text, words text[]) RETURNS SETOF public.songs
    LANGUAGE sql
    AS $$   
select id, name, artist
from songs s
where lower(name) like concat(lower(_name), '%') and 
		lower(artist) like concat(lower(_artist), '%') 
		and (array_length(words,1) is null or
		exists (select * 
			   from words_in_songs w
			   where w.word = Any(words) 
				and song_id =s.id
			   ))
$$;


ALTER FUNCTION public.filtersongs(_name text, _artist text, words text[]) OWNER TO postgres;

--
-- TOC entry 252 (class 1255 OID 16969)
-- Name: get_all_instances(); Type: FUNCTION; Schema: public; Owner: postgres
--

CREATE FUNCTION public.get_all_instances() RETURNS SETOF public.instance
    LANGUAGE sql
    AS $$select word, song_id, s.name, s.artist, w.paragraph,w.line_index, w.total_line_index, w.inline_index
from public.words_in_songs as w
join public.songs s on w.song_id = s.id
order by word$$;

--
-- TOC entry 243 (class 1255 OID 16799)
-- Name: get_line(bigint, integer); Type: FUNCTION; Schema: public; Owner: postgres
--

CREATE FUNCTION public.get_line(songid bigint, line integer) RETURNS SETOF public.lyrics_element
    LANGUAGE sql
    AS $$select element, type
from
	(SELECT word as element, index, song_id, 'word' as type
		FROM public.words_in_songs
		where song_id=songid and total_line_index=line
		union (
			select mark as element,index,song_id, 'mark' as type
			from public.marks_in_songs 
			where type='punctuation' and song_id=songid and total_line_index=line )
	order by index) as elements
	$$;


ALTER FUNCTION public.get_line(songid bigint, line integer) OWNER TO postgres;

--
-- TOC entry 248 (class 1255 OID 16841)
-- Name: get_lines_lengths(); Type: FUNCTION; Schema: public; Owner: postgres
--

CREATE FUNCTION public.get_lines_lengths() RETURNS SETOF public.stat
    LANGUAGE sql
    AS $$select words_in_lines, count(*) as num_of_lines
from (select song_id, total_line_index, count(*) as words_in_lines
	from words_in_songs
	group by song_id, total_line_index) a
group by words_in_lines
order by num_of_lines desc
limit 8$$;


ALTER FUNCTION public.get_lines_lengths() OWNER TO postgres;

--
-- TOC entry 244 (class 1255 OID 16842)
-- Name: get_paragraphs_lengths(); Type: FUNCTION; Schema: public; Owner: postgres
--

CREATE FUNCTION public.get_paragraphs_lengths() RETURNS SETOF public.stat
    LANGUAGE sql
    AS $$select words_in_paragraphs, count(*) as num_of_paragraphs
from (select song_id, paragraph, count(*) as words_in_paragraphs
	from words_in_songs
	group by song_id, paragraph) a
group by words_in_paragraphs
order by num_of_paragraphs desc
limit 8$$;


ALTER FUNCTION public.get_paragraphs_lengths() OWNER TO postgres;

    LANGUAGE sql
    AS $$

	$$;

--

CREATE FUNCTION public.get_word_instances(_word text) RETURNS SETOF public.word_instance
    LANGUAGE sql
    AS $$select distinct song_id, s.name, s.artist, w.paragraph,w.line_index, w.total_line_index, w.inline_index
from public.words_in_songs as w
join public.songs s on w.song_id = s.id
where lower(word)=lower(_word)$$;

-- TOC entry 246 (class 1255 OID 16847)
-- Name: get_words_counts(); Type: FUNCTION; Schema: public; Owner: postgres
--

CREATE FUNCTION public.get_words_counts() RETURNS SETOF public.word_count
    LANGUAGE sql
    AS $$select lower(word) as lowerWord, count(*) as instances
from words_in_songs
group by lowerWord
order by instances desc
limit 8
$$;


ALTER FUNCTION public.get_words_counts() OWNER TO postgres;

--
-- TOC entry 247 (class 1255 OID 16838)
-- Name: get_words_lengths(); Type: FUNCTION; Schema: public; Owner: postgres
--

CREATE FUNCTION public.get_words_lengths() RETURNS SETOF public.stat
    LANGUAGE sql
    AS $$select cast(char_length(word) as bigint),count(*) as num
from words_in_songs
group by char_length(word)
order by num desc
limit 8$$;
